<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похитить.html>похи́тить</a> (5705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-хи́тить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-xítitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похитить.html>похи́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxítitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похищать.html>похища́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to abduct, to kidnap</li>
<li>to purloin, to steal</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похищение.html>похище́ние</a> (9580)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похитить.html>похи́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poxítitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похищение.html>похище́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxiščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похищение.html>похище́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похищение.html>похище́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похищение.html>похище́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>theft, kidnapping, abduction, hijacking</li></ol>

***похлопать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похлопать.html>похло́пать</a> (5252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлопать.html>хло́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlópatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похлопать.html>похло́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxlópatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to slap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:похлопать.html>похло́пать</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плечу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxlópatʹ</b> kovó-libo po plečú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to clap/tap/pat someone on the shoulder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give a clap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:похлопать.html>похло́паем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́стю</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vse <b>poxlópajem</b> góstju!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">give the guest a clap, everyone!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́дов</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> campaign, march</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cruise</li>
<li>trip, walking tour, hike
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́д</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xodítʹ v <b>poxód</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hike</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>tour</li></ol>

***походить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:походить.html>походи́ть</a> (2887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:походить.html>походи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to look like, to resemble</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:походить.html>походи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to walk <i>(for a while)</i></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походить.html>Походи́ть</a></b> is in the class of Russian abstract verbs. Its counterparts, <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a>, are concrete verbs.
</p>

***походный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дный</a> (8897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поход.html>похо́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poxód</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxódnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> march, marching, route
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порядок.html>поря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnyj</b> porjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">marching order; march formation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>строй</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnyj</b> stroj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">march formation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:песня.html>пе́сня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnaja</b> pésnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">marching song</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:колонна.html>коло́нна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnaja</b> kolónna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">column of route</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> field, camp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnaja</b> krovátʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">camp bed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:снаряжение.html>снаряже́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnoje</b> snarjažénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">field kit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnaja</b> fórma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">marching order; field dress</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> field, mobile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:госпиталь.html>го́спиталь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnyj</b> góspitalʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">field hospital</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:походный.html>похо́дная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кухня.html>ку́хня</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxódnaja</b> kúxnja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">mobile kitchen; field kitchen</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похолодание.html>похолода́ние</a> (29281)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодать.html>похолода́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">poxolodátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодание.html>похолода́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxolodánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодание.html>похолода́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодание.html>похолода́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодание.html>похолода́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cooling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the weather</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, cold snap, cold spell</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cooling, worsening <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of relations between people</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похолодать.html>похолода́ть</a> (26280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">холода́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xolodátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похолодать.html>похолода́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxolodátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">холода́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become colder <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the weather</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become cold or colder</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to suffer from the cold, to shiver, to get chilled</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похоронить.html>похорони́ть</a> (4512)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоронить.html>хорони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xoronítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похоронить.html>похорони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxoronítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хоронить.html>хорони́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bury, to inter</li>
<li><i>obsolete,colloquial</i> to hide, to conceal, to lay away</li></ol>

***похоронный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похоронный.html>похоро́нный</a> (9338)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похороны.html>по́хороны</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póxorony</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похоронный.html>похоро́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxorónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> funeral; funerary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:похоронный.html>похоро́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poxorónnyj</b> marš</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>funeral</b> march</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> somber, sad</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похоть.html>по́хоть</a> (21434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хоте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xotétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to want</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похоть.html>по́хоть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">póxotʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похоть.html>по́хоти</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)

<ol><li>lust</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:похудевший.html>похуде́вший</a> (8599)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похудевший.html>похуде́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxudévšij</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:худеть.html>худе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xudétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:похудеть.html>похуде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poxudétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:худеть.html>худе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow thin, to lose weight</li></ol>
